>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">子句1: </span></span> $¬gt(x,y)∨¬gt(y,z)∨gt(x,z)$
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">替换 </span></span> $x=5,y=3$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，得到 </span></span> $¬gt(3,z)∨gt(5,z)$
>
> 7.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">从新子句 </span></span>$¬gt(3,z)∨gt(5,z)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 和 </span></span>$gt(3,2)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：归结出 </span></span>$gt(5,2)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">替换 </span></span> $z=2$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">， </span></span> $¬gt(3,2)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 与 </span></span> $gt(3,2)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 互补，得到 </span></span> $gt(5,2)$
>
> 8.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">从 </span></span> $gt(5,2)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 和目标子句 </span></span> $¬gt(5,2)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：归结出空子句，证明完成。</span></span>
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">因此，正确的证明不需要自反性公理，而是需要后继事实和传递性公理，通过一系列归结步骤推导出矛盾。</span></span>

***

```
第六节课 13.0_Belief_Networks
```

> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">本课的核心是：当世界不确定时，我们如何用</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概率</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">来表示知识，并用</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">贝叶斯网络</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">来进行高效的推理。内容可分为四大模块：</span></span>
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概率推理基础</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：为什么需要概率，以及概率论的基本概念。</span></span>
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">贝叶斯网络</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：如何用图模型紧凑地表示复杂的联合概率分布。</span></span>
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">精确推理</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：如何在网络中进行精确的概率计算（枚举法、变量消除法）。</span></span>
>
> 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">近似推理</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：当网络太大太复杂时，如何用采样方法得到近似解（随机模拟）。</span></span>

# **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">一. 为什么要用概率？（不确定性）</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心问题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：逻辑智能体（命题逻辑、一阶逻辑）在真实世界中太“脆弱”，因为它们要求绝对的真或假。真实世界充满了：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">部分可观测性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">（不知道其他司机的计划）</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">噪声传感器</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">（交通报告可能不准）</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">不确定的行动结果</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">（可能会爆胎）</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">建模的复杂性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">（无法枚举所有情况）</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">逻辑方法的缺陷</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">结论过于绝对，可能错误。（“25分钟一定能到机场”）</span></span>
    *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">结论过于保守，无法决策。（“25分钟能到，如果不出任何意外...”）</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概率方法的优势</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：提供了一种</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">量化的信念度</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>`P(A25 | 无事故) = 0.04`。

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考试可能考察</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简答题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：比较逻辑推理与概率推理的优缺点，并举例说明。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">选择题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：给定一个场景，判断其不确定性来源。</span></span>

> ```
> 核心驱动力：为什么需要概率？
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">想象两个场景：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">场景A（逻辑世界）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：你的朋友问：“如果我现在出门，能赶上8点的电影吗？”你基于“路程20分钟”的规则回答：“能。”结果路上摔了一跤，没赶上。你的回答</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">错了</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">场景B（概率世界）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：同一个问题，你回答：“根据当前路况和历史数据，你准时到的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概率是85%</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。” 这个回答</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">更诚实、更有用</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，因为它包含了不确定性。</span></span>
>
> ![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="N5V4BC52" width="1208" height="503" src="attachments/N5V4BC52.png" ztype="zimage"> | 1208](attachments/N5V4BC52.png)
>
> ![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="Y4B9WEV5" width="1222" height="509" src="attachments/Y4B9WEV5.png" ztype="zimage"> | 1222](attachments/Y4B9WEV5.png)
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">课件PPT5和6的核心思想就是：真实世界像场景B，充满了未知和意外。逻辑（True/False）太脆弱，无法处理这些不确定性。概率（0到1之间的一个数）为我们提供了描述这种不确定性的语言。</span></span>**
>
> ```
> 概率是什么？一种“信念度”
> ```
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">不是频率</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：并不是说你出发100次，只有4次能赶上飞机（虽然有时可以这样理解）。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">是主观信念（贝叶斯观点）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">基于你当前掌握的所有信息</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，你对“A25能准时到”这个命题的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">相信程度</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">是0.04。当新信息到来（如“听说前方有事故”），你的信念度（概率）会动态更新。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">就像逻辑蕴含的“软版本”</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：逻辑说“KB蕴含α，所以α必然为真”。概率说“KB支持α，所以α为真的信念度是0.9”。</span></span>

# **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">二. 概率论基础</span></span>**

<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这是后续所有内容的数学基石，必须掌握。</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 条件概率与贝叶斯规则</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">条件概率</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>$P(a|b)$ 在已知b发生的情况下，a发生的概率。

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">定义</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $P(a|b) = P(a ∧ b) / P(b)$

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">乘积规则</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $P(a ∧ b) = P(a|b) P(b) = P(b|a) P(a)$

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">贝叶斯规则</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：由乘积规则推导而来，是</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">因果推理</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">到</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">诊断推理</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的桥梁。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">公式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $P(Cause|Effect) = [P(Effect|Cause) * P(Cause)] / P(Effect)$

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">例子（脑膜炎）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

        *   $P(m|s) = [P(s|m) * P(m)] / P(s) = [0.8 * 0.0001] / 0.1 = 0.0008$

        *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">关键洞见</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：即使脖子僵硬由脑膜炎引起的概率很高(0.8)，但得脑膜炎的先验概率极低(0.0001)，导致后验概率仍然很小(0.0008)。这解释了为什么医生不会一看到某个症状就断定是罕见病。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考试可能考察</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：直接应用贝叶斯规则进行计算（如上例）。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概念题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：解释贝叶斯规则在诊断问题中的作用。</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 独立性与条件独立性</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">独立性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：如果A和B独立，则 </span></span>$P(A|B) = P(A)$ 或 $P(A,B) = P(A)P(B)$。

    *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">强大但</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">很罕见</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">条件独立性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：在给定另一个变量C时，A和B独立。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">公式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $P(A,B|C) = P(A|C) P(B|C)$

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">例子（牙医）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $牙痛(Toothache)$  和  $探针卡住(Catch)$  在给定  $蛀牙(Cavity)$  时是条件独立的。也就是说，如果已经知道有蛀牙，那么探针是否卡住就不受牙痛这个信息影响了。

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">威力</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：是贝叶斯网络能够</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简化模型</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的关键。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考试可能考察</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">判断题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：判断两个变量在给定某组证据下是否条件独立。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简答题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：解释条件独立性如何帮助减少概率模型所需的参数数量。</span></span>

> ```
> 概率的基石：必须掌握的三个规则
> ```
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 条件概率 - “新信息如何改变我的信念”</span></span>**
>
> *   $P(蛀牙|牙痛) = 0.8$  **不代表** “牙痛会导致蛀牙”。
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">它的真实含义是：</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">在我目前只知道“你牙痛”这一信息的情况下</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，我对“你有蛀牙”的信念度是0.8。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">如果</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">随后通过X光确认了有蛀牙，那么概率就变成了1。但之前基于部分信息的判断（0.8）在它自己的信息背景下依然是有效的。</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 乘积规则 - “同时发生的概率”</span></span>**
>
> *   $P(A且B) = P(A|B) * P(B)$
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">把“A且B”分解成两步：先看B发生的概率，再看在B发生的情况下A也发生的概率。</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">c) 贝叶斯规则 - “从结果反推原因”</span></span>**
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这是</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">最重要的规则之一</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">公式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $P(原因|结果) = [P(结果|原因) * P(原因)] / P(结果)$
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">为什么有用</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：我们通常更容易知道“原因导致结果”的概率，但真正想知道的是“看到结果，反推原因”的概率。</span></span>
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">例子（脑膜炎）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
>         *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">医生知道：</span></span> $P(脖子僵硬|脑膜炎) = 0.8$  （因果概率，容易从医学知识得到）
>
>         *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">医生想知道：</span></span> $P(脑膜炎|脖子僵硬)$  （诊断概率，这才是诊断需要的）
>
>         *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">贝叶斯规则将两者联系起来。计算后发现，即使脖子僵硬由脑膜炎引起概率很高(0.8)，但因为脑膜炎本身太罕见(P=0.0001)，所以最终诊断概率仍然很低(P=0.0008)。</span></span>
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">深刻洞见</span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">：贝叶斯规则</span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">自然地结合了先验知识（疾病的普遍性）和新证据（症状）</span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">。</span>
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 威力巨大的概念：条件独立性
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这是理解后续贝叶斯网络为何高效的关键。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">独立性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：知道B与否，完全不影响我对A的信念。</span></span> $P(A|B) = P(A)$ 。**这在现实世界中非常罕见**。
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">条件独立性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：在</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">给定第三个变量C</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的情况下，A和B变得独立。</span></span>
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">经典例子（牙医）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
>         *   `牙痛` 和 `探针卡住` 一般来说是相关的（如果一个发生，另一个也更可能发生）。
>
>         *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">但是</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，如果我们</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">已经知道</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">你有</span></span>`蛀牙`，那么`牙痛`这个信息就不再能提供任何关于`探针是否会卡住`的新信息了！因为蛀牙本身就是导致两者发生的共同原因。
>
>         *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">用数学表达：</span></span> $P(探针卡住 | 蛀牙, 牙痛) = P(探针卡住 | 蛀牙)$
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">带来的好处</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：大幅简化计算。联合分布 </span></span> $P(牙痛, 探针, 蛀牙)$  原本需要7个独立参数，利用条件独立性后，只需要  $P(牙痛|蛀牙)$ 、 $P(探针|蛀牙)$ 、 $P(蛀牙)$  这 **2+2+1=5** 个参数。
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> Wumpus世界的概率推理
> ```
>
> ![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="Q8RNGUJ5" width="1221" height="484" src="attachments/Q8RNGUJ5.png" ztype="zimage"> | 1221](attachments/Q8RNGUJ5.png)
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这展示了如何将概率应用于一个具体问题。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">问题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：在已知某些格子有微风、某些格子安全的情况下，推断未知格子有陷阱的概率是多少？</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">暴力方法（枚举）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：考虑所有可能的陷阱分布组合，计算哪种组合与我们的观察（微风模式）最一致。</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算量随格子数指数增长，不可行</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">聪明方法（利用条件独立性）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：发现一个格子的微风</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">只取决于它相邻的格子</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，与远处格子无关。这正是一种</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">条件独立性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。利用这一点，可以</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">局部地</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算概率，极大地降低了计算复杂度，使得推理变得可行。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">结果</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：计算出的概率（如[1,3]格有陷阱的概率是31%，[2,2]格是86%）为智能体的决策提供了量化依据，比单纯的猜测要强大得多。</span></span>
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 总结与考试建议
> ```
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">拥抱不确定性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：概率不是妥协，而是对复杂世界的诚实和精确的描述。</span></span>
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">理解贝叶斯规则</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：学会从“因果”思维切换到“诊断”思维，并理解先验知识的重要性。</span></span>
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">掌握条件独立性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这是将复杂问题变简单的“魔法钥匙”。它的核心思想是：</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">如果知道了某个共同原因，那么其不同的结果之间可能就不再相互提供新的信息了。</span></span>**
>
> 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Wumpus例子是桥梁</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：它展示了概率推理如何解决实际问题，并为接下来学习更强大的工具——</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">贝叶斯网络</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">——打下了坚实的基础。</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考试中，这部分是基础，可能会考察：</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概念解释</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：什么是条件概率？贝叶斯规则的意义是什么？</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：直接应用贝叶斯规则、条件概率公式进行计算。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简答题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：为什么条件独立性很重要？并用例子说明。</span></span>

# **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">三. 贝叶斯网络</span></span><span style="color: rgb(255, 32, 32)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">（重要）</span></span>**

<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这是本章的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心与灵魂</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">是什么</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：一个</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">有向无环图</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，其中：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">节点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = 随机变量。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">边</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = 直接的因果或影响关系。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">每个节点的条件概率表</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = 在给定其父节点取值时，该节点取不同值的概率。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">全局语义</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：整个网络的联合概率分布是每个节点给定其父节点条件概率的乘积。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">公式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $P(X_1, X_2, ..., X_n) = \prod P(X_i | Parents(X_i))$

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">例子（警报网络）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：<br></span></span> $P(J, M, A, ¬B, ¬E) = P(J|A) * P(M|A) * P(A|¬B,¬E) * P(¬B) * P(¬E)$

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">紧凑性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：对于n个布尔变量，联合分布需要</span></span> $O(2^n)$ 个参数，而一个父节点数不超过k的贝叶斯网络只需要 $O(n * 2^k)$ 个参数。从指数级降到线性级。

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考试可能考察</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">画图题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：根据一段文字描述，画出对应的贝叶斯网络结构。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：给定一个小的贝叶斯网络和CPT，计算某个联合概率或条件概率。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简答题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：解释为什么贝叶斯网络能够紧凑地表示联合概率分布。</span></span>

> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这部分内容是整个概率推理的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">高潮</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。它介绍了一个极其强大的工具——</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">贝叶斯网络</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，它能将我们之前学到的所有概率概念（联合分布、条件概率、条件独立性）用一种直观的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">图模型</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">封装起来。</span></span>
>
> ```
> 贝叶斯网络是什么？一个“概率地图”
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">想象一下，你要向别人解释为什么你会迟到。你可能会画一个这样的示意图：</span></span>
>
> ![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="3LKRJ9HC" width="671" height="285" src="attachments/3LKRJ9HC.png" ztype="zimage"> | 671](attachments/3LKRJ9HC.png)
>
> ```
> [下雨] -> [堵车] -> [迟到]
> [闹钟坏了] -> [晚起] -> [迟到]
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这个图描述了事件之间的因果关系。贝叶斯网络就是这种思路的数学化和精确化。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">它是一个图</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">节点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：你关心的随机变量（如 </span></span>`窃贼`、`地震`、`报警器`）。
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">有向边</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：从“原因”指向“结果”（如 </span></span>`窃贼` -> `报警器`）。
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">禁止循环</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：不能有“A导致B，B又导致A”的循环，因为这会导致逻辑混乱。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">每个节点附带一个“小说明书”</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这个“说明书”就是</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">条件概率表</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">它精确描述了：</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">在父节点各种不同状态组合下，这个节点取不同值的概率是多少</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">例如，</span></span>`报警器` 节点的CPT告诉你：当 `窃贼=true` 且 `地震=false` 时，报警器响的概率是0.94；当 `窃贼=false` 且 `地震=false` 时，报警器响的概率是0.001。![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="FN9AZS5W" width="1083" height="521" src="attachments/FN9AZS5W.png" ztype="zimage"> | 1083](attachments/FN9AZS5W.png)
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 为什么贝叶斯网络如此强大？
> ```
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 惊人的紧凑性</span></span>**
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这是贝叶斯网络最大的优势之一。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">暴力方法（联合分布）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：要描述5个布尔变量的世界，你需要 </span></span> $2^5 = 32$  个概率数字。这就像记住一张有32个条目的巨大表格。
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">贝叶斯网络方法</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过利用变量间的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">条件独立性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，你只需要记住</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">少得多的数字</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">在盗窃网络中，你只需要 </span></span> $10$  个数字！
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">原理</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：你不需要为每一个可能的世界配置都存储一个概率。你只需要存储那些局部的、因果性的规则（CPT）。整个世界的概率可以通过把这些局部规则</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">乘起来</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">得到（全局语义）。</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简单类比</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">联合分布</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：像背一本电话簿，需要记住每一个人的号码。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">贝叶斯网络</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：像掌握加法规则，只需要知道基本规则，就能算出任何数的和。</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 直观的语义</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">全局语义</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $P(世界状态) = \prod P(局部效果 | 局部原因)$ 。整个网络的联合概率等于所有节点条件概率的乘积。这为我们**计算任何事件的概率**提供了公式。
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">局部语义</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：每个节点只关心它的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">父节点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。在给定父节点之后，这个节点就和它的“叔叔伯伯”（非后代节点）没关系了。这使得推理可以</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">局部化</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，非常符合直觉。</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">c) 马尔可夫毯：终极的“隔离罩”</span></span>**
>
> ![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="GTLNKSIQ" width="1113" height="413" src="attachments/GTLNKSIQ.png" ztype="zimage"> | 1113](attachments/GTLNKSIQ.png)
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">是什么</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：一个节点的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">父节点 + 子节点 + 子节点的其他父节点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">威力</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">一旦你知道了一个节点的马尔可夫毯，这个网络中的其他任何节点都无法带给你关于这个节点的任何新信息。</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">例子</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：要预测 </span></span>`报警器`，你只需要知道：
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">它的原因（父节点：</span></span>`窃贼`、`地震`）。
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">它的结果（子节点：</span></span>`约翰打电话`、`玛丽打电话`）。
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">以及它结果的其它原因（</span></span>`约翰打电话` 和 `玛丽打电话` 没有其他父节点，所以这部分为空）。
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">因此，</span></span>`报警器` 的马尔可夫毯就是 {`窃贼`, `地震`, `约翰打电话`, `玛丽打电话`}。知道了这些，像“今天星期几”这种信息就和 `报警器` 无关了。
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 如何构建一个“好”的网络？
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">课件通过一个反例（</span></span>$M, J, A, B, E$ 顺序）说明了**构建顺序至关重要**。
>
> ![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="QK4QP7FV" width="1211" height="460" src="attachments/QK4QP7FV.png" ztype="zimage"> | 1211](attachments/QK4QP7FV.png)
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">最佳实践：遵循因果顺序</span></span>**
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">先列出根本原因（</span></span>`窃贼`、`地震`）。
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">再列出它们导致的中层事件（</span></span>`报警器`）。
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">最后列出观察到的现象（</span></span>`约翰打电话`、`玛丽打电话`）。
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">为什么？</span></span>**
>
>     1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">符合直觉</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：我们更容易思考和评估“在有窃贼时，报警器响的概率”（</span></span> $P(A|B)$ ），而不是“在约翰和玛丽都打电话时，有窃贼的概率”（ $P(B|J,M)$ ），尽管后者可以通过贝叶斯规则计算。
>
>     2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">更紧凑</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：因果顺序通常会产生最少的边和最少的参数。反过来的顺序会导致网络结构复杂，需要更多的概率数字。</span></span>
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 扩展：处理连续变量
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">现实世界不只有“是/否”。贝叶斯网络可以处理连续变量（如</span></span>`成本`、`收成`）。
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">思路</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：不再使用CPT，而是使用</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概率分布函数</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">线性高斯模型</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：用于子节点是连续变量的情况。它假设子节点的值围绕着一个由父节点值决定的均值呈高斯分布。</span></span>
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Probit分布</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：用于父节点是连续变量，子节点是离散变量（如</span></span>`是否购买`）的情况。它提供了一个平滑的、S形的概率阈值。
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 总结与考试建议
> ```
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">贝叶斯网络是“概率地图”</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：用图表示变量间的因果关系，用CPT表示影响强度。</span></span>
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心威力是紧凑性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过条件独立性，用线性增长的数字描述指数级复杂的世界。</span></span>
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">记住两个语义</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">全局</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：联合概率 = 所有CPT条目相乘。</span></span>
>
>     *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">局部</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：每个节点只受父节点直接影响。</span></span>
>
> 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">按因果顺序构建</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这样最自然、最简单、最高效。</span></span>
>
> 5.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">马尔可夫毯是推理的关键</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：它界定了一个节点的“信息影响圈”。</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 102, 102, 0.5)">考试中，这部分是绝对的重点，可能会考察：</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">画图题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：给一段文字描述，画出对应的贝叶斯网络结构。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：给定一个小型网络的CPT，计算某个联合概率或条件概率。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概念题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：解释为什么贝叶斯网络是紧凑的？什么是局部语义/全局语义？马尔可夫毯是什么？</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">比较题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：比较不同变量顺序下构建的网络复杂度和自然度。</span></span>

# **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">四. 推理任务</span></span>**

<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">在贝叶斯网络中，我们主要进行以下几种推理：</span></span>

1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简单查询</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：计算后验边际概率 </span></span> $P(查询变量 | 证据)$ 。例如： $P(盗窃 | 约翰打电话，玛丽没打电话)$ 。

2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">联结查询</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $P(X, Y | E)$ 。

3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">最优决策</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：结合效用理论。</span></span>

4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">信息价值</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：下一步应该观察哪个变量？</span></span>

> ```
> 推理的“菜谱”：我们要解决什么问题？
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">推理不仅仅是计算一个概率。它是一整套用于</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">智能决策</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的工具箱：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简单查询（最基础）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：“现在我知道约翰和玛丽都打电话了(</span></span> $j,m$ )，那发生入室盗窃( $B$ )的概率是多少？” ->  $P(B|j,m)$
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">决策</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：“我应该提前90分钟还是120分钟出发？” 这需要将概率 </span></span> $P(准时到达)$  与不同结果的**效用**（快乐/成本）结合起来。
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">信息价值</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：“我是该先检查地震报告，还是先打电话给邻居？” 推理可以帮助判断哪个信息能最大程度减少不确定性。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">解释</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：“为什么AI诊断系统认为我的启动马达坏了？” 推理过程可以追溯出最可能的原因。</span></span>

# **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">五. 精确推理算法</span></span>**

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 枚举法</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">思路</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过固定证据变量，对隐藏变量求和，来回答查询。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">问题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算复杂度高</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> (</span></span>`O(d^n)`)，效率低下，因为存在大量重复计算。

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 变量消除法</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">思路</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">从右到左进行求和</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，并</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缓存中间结果（因子）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 来避免重复计算。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">过程</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：重新排列求和项，逐步求和消除变量，并在过程中进行因子的点积。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：比枚举法高效得多。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">关键优化</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：识别</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">无关变量</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">定理</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：一个变量与查询在给定证据下是</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">d-分离</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的，那么它就是无关变量。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考试可能考察</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">应用题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：给定一个小型网络和查询，使用变量消除法分步计算后验概率。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概念题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：比较枚举法和变量消除法的效率。</span></span>

> ```
> 精确推理：从“蛮力”到“聪明”的求和
> ```
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 枚举法 - “基础款”</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">思路</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：要算 </span></span> $P(B|j,m)$ ，就把所有能让  $B$  为真，且满足  $j,m$  的可能世界都找出来，把它们的概率加起来。
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">做法</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：利用联合概率=CPT乘积的全局语义，列出公式 </span></span> $P(B|j,m) = α Σ_e Σ_a P(B)P(e)P(a|B,e)P(j|a)P(m|a)$ 。
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">像暴力破解</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，存在大量重复计算，效率低。</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 变量消除法 - “优化版”</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">思路</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">从右往左算，边算边存</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心技巧</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
>     1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">因子</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：把求和过程中的中间结果存起来（比如 </span></span> $f_J(a) = P(j|a)$ ）。
>
>     2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除顺序</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：明智地选择先对哪个变量求和。</span></span>
>
>     3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">识别无关变量</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：用 </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">m-分离</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 准则判断哪些变量根本不需要考虑，直接忽略。</span></span>
>
>         *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">例子</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：问 </span></span> $P(JohnCalls|Alarm=true)$ ， $Burglary$  和  $Earthquake$  都被 Alarm **挡住**了，成为无关变量，计算时完全不用管它们。这大大简化了问题。
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：比枚举法快得多，是精确推理的实用算法。</span></span>

***

> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">第一次作业中的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(126, 131, 134)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">问题3: 贝叶斯网络与变量消除</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">是属于这一部分的知识，我们来通过这道题加深一下对于贝叶斯网络和变量消除这部分知识的理解</span></span>
>
> ```
> 原题目
> ```
>
> ![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="Y4FKYVES" width="1698" height="868" src="attachments/Y4FKYVES.png" ztype="zimage"> | 1698](attachments/Y4FKYVES.png)  
>
> ```
> 题目翻译解析
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">关键要求部分翻译：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考虑下面给出的贝叶斯网络，所有变量都是布尔值的。展示变量消除过程对于以下情况：</span></span>
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">对于左图，计算 </span></span> $P(X_3∣X_4)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，消除顺序为 </span></span> $X_5​, X_1​, X_2$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​</span></span>
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">对于左图，计算 </span></span> $P(X_3∣X_4)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，消除顺序为 </span></span> $X_2​, X_1​, X_5$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​</span></span>
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">对于右图，计算 </span></span> $P(X_3∣X_4)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，消除顺序为 </span></span> $X_5​, X_1​, X_2$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​</span></span>
>
>     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">对于右图，计算 </span></span> $P(X_3∣X_4)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，消除顺序为 </span></span> $X_2​, X_1​, X_5$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​</span></span>
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">专有名词翻译：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Bayesian network：贝叶斯网络</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Variable elimination：变量消除</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Boolean：布尔值</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Order of elimination：消除顺序</span></span>
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 关键知识点回顾与解题思路构建
> ```
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">关键知识点回顾：</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">变量消除（Variable Elimination）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：是一种用于贝叶斯网络推理的算法，通过逐步消除变量来计算查询概率。消除顺序影响计算效率。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">贝叶斯网络</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：由有向无环图表示，每个节点对应一个变量，条件概率表（CPT）定义给定父节点下变量的概率。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">条件概率计算</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：为了计算 </span></span> $P(X∣Y)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，我们使用变量消除来边缘化其他变量。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除顺序</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：选择不同的消除顺序可能会导致不同的计算复杂度，但最终结果相同。</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">解题思路构建：</span></span>**
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">对于左图和右图的贝叶斯网络，计算条件概率 </span></span>$P(X_3∣X_4)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 使用变量消除法。所有变量均为布尔类型。变量消除过程基于给定的消除顺序，逐步消除非查询非证据变量，最终得到 </span></span>$P(X_3,X_4)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，然后通过归一化得到 </span></span>$P(X_3∣X_4)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。以下是详细过程。</span></span>![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="6GLDFUU7" width="1044" height="351" src="attachments/6GLDFUU7.png" ztype="zimage"> | 1044](attachments/6GLDFUU7.png)
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 详细解题步骤
> ```
>
> ### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">左图贝叶斯网络结构</span></span>**
>
> ![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="PEYEB2GR" width="421" height="384" src="attachments/PEYEB2GR.png" ztype="zimage"> | 421](attachments/PEYEB2GR.png)
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">联合概率分布为：</span></span>
>
> $$
> P(X_1,X_2,X_3,X_4,X_5)=P(X_1)⋅P(X_3∣X_1)⋅P(X_2∣X_1,X_3)⋅P(X_4∣X_2)⋅P(X_5∣X_2)
> $$
>
> **消除顺序：**$X_5,X_1,X_2​$
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$X_5$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_5$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 的因子： </span></span>$P(X_5∣X_2)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{5}\left(X_{2}\right)=\sum_{X_{5}} P\left(X_{5} \mid X_{2}\right)=1
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">由于 </span></span>$\tau_{5}\left(X_{2}\right)=1$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 是常数，可以忽略。<br>剩余因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right), P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right)$
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$X_{1}$**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_{1}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 的因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{2}\right)=\sum_{X_{1}} P\left(X_{1}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">剩余因子： </span></span>$\tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{2}\right), P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right)$
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$X_{2}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_{2}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 的因子： </span></span>$\tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{2}\right), P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)=\sum_{X_{2}} \tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{2}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     $\tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 即为 </span></span>$P\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。<br>然后 </span></span>$P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{4}\right)=\frac{\tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)}{\sum_{X_{3}} \tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)}  $<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​。</span></span>
>
> **消除顺序：**$X_{2}, X_{1}, X_{5}$
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$X_{2}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_{2}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 的因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right), P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right), P\left(X_{5} \mid X_{2}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{2}\left(X_{1}, X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}\right)=\sum_{X_{2}} P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{5} \mid X_{2}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">剩余因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right), \tau_{2}\left(X_{1}, X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}\right)$
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$X_{1}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_{1}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 的因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right), \tau_{2}\left(X_{1}, X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}\right)=\sum_{X_{1}} P\left(X_{1}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right) \cdot \tau_{2}\left(X_{1}, X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">剩余因子： </span></span>$\tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}\right)$
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$X_{5}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_{5}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 的因子： </span></span>$\tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)=\sum_{X_{5}} \tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     $\tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 即为 </span></span>$P\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。<br>然后 </span></span>$P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{4}\right)=\frac{\tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)}{\sum_{X_{3}} \tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
> ### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">右图贝叶斯网络结构</span></span>**
>
> ![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="2PEARPI4" width="505" height="395" src="attachments/2PEARPI4.png" ztype="zimage"> | 505](attachments/2PEARPI4.png)
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">联合概率分布为：</span></span>
>
> $$
> P(X_1,X_2,X_3,X_4,X_5,X_6)=P(X_1)⋅P(X_3∣X_1)⋅P(X_2∣X_1,X_3)⋅P(X_4∣X_2)⋅P(X_5∣X_2,X_6)⋅P(X_6)
> $$
>
> **消除顺序：**$X_5,X_1,X_2$
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$ X_{5}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_{5}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 的因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{5} \mid X_{2}, X_{6}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{5}\left(X_{2}, X_{6}\right)=\sum_{X_{5}} P\left(X_{5} \mid X_{2}, X_{6}\right)=1
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">由于 </span></span>$\tau_{5}\left(X_{2}, X_{6}\right)=1$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 是常数，可以忽略。<br>剩余因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right), P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right), P\left(X_{6}\right)$
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$X_{1}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_{1}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 的因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{2}\right)=\sum_{X_{1}} P\left(X_{1}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">剩余因子： </span></span>$\tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{2}\right), P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right), P\left(X_{6}\right)$
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$X_{2}$**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_{2}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 的因子： </span></span>$\tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{2}\right), P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)=\sum_{X_{2}} \tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{2}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">剩余因子： </span></span>$\tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right), P\left(X_{6}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>为了得到 </span></span>$P\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，需要对 </span></span>$X_{6}$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">求和：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     P\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)=\sum_{X_{6}} \tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{6}\right)=\tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right) \cdot \sum_{X_{6}} P\left(X_{6}\right)=\tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">因此 </span></span>$\tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 即为 </span></span>$P\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。<br>然后 </span></span>$P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{4}\right)=\frac{\tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)}{\sum_{X_{3}} \tau_{2}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​。</span></span>
>
> **消除顺序：**$X_2,X_1,X_5$
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$X_{2}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_{2}$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right), P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right), P\left(X_{5} \mid X_{2}, X_{6}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{2}\left(X_{1}, X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}, X_{6}\right)=\sum_{X_{2}} P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{5} \mid X_{2}, X_{6}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">剩余因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right), \tau_{2}\left(X_{1}, X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}, X_{6}\right), P\left(X_{6}\right)$
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$X_{1}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$X_{1}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 的因子： </span></span>$P\left(X_{1}\right), P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right), \tau_{2}\left(X_{1}, X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}, X_{6}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}, X_{6}\right)=\sum_{X_{1}} P\left(X_{1}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right) \cdot \tau_{2}\left(X_{1}, X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}, X_{6}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">剩余因子： </span></span>$\tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}, X_{6}\right), P\left(X_{6}\right)$
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">消除 </span></span>**$ X_{5}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>包含 </span></span>$ X_{5}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 的因子： </span></span>$\tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}, X_{6}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>计算：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     \tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)=\sum_{X_{5}} \tau_{1}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}, X_{5}, X_{6}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">注意：由于 </span></span>$\sum_{X_{5}} P\left(X_{5} \mid X_{2}, X_{6}\right)=1$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，因此 </span></span>$\tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 不依赖于 </span></span>$X_{6}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​，即 </span></span>$\tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)= \sum_{X_{1}} P\left(X_{1}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{1}\right) \cdot \sum_{X_{2}} P\left(X_{2} \mid X_{1}, X_{3}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{4} \mid X_{2}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。<br>剩余因子： </span></span>$\tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right), P\left(X_{6}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br>为了得到 </span></span>$P\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，需要对 </span></span>$X_{6}$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​ 求和：</span></span>
>
>     $$
>     P\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)=\sum_{X_{6}} \tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right) \cdot P\left(X_{6}\right)=\tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right) \cdot \sum_{X_{6}} P\left(X_{6}\right)=\tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)
>
>     $$
>
>     <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">因此 </span></span>$\tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 即为 </span></span>$P\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。<br>然后 </span></span>$P\left(X_{3} \mid X_{4}\right)=\frac{\tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)}{\sum_{X_{3}} \tau_{3}\left(X_{3}, X_{4}\right)}  。$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">​。</span></span>
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">以上为变量消除的详细过程。最终的条件概率 </span></span>$P(X_3∣X_4)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 需通过归一化 </span></span>$P(X_3,X_4)P(X_3​,X_4​)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 得到。</span></span>

# **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">六. 近似推理算法</span></span>**

<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">当网络太大，精确推理不可行时，我们使用采样方法。</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 拒绝采样</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">过程</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：根据先验分布生成样本，然后拒绝所有与证据不匹配的样本，在剩余的样本中统计查询变量的比例。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：如果证据 </span></span>`P(e)` 的概率很小，绝大多数样本都会被拒绝，**效率极低**。

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 似然加权采样</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">过程</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：固定证据变量的值，只对非证据变量采样。每个样本赋予一个</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">权重</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，权重是证据变量按其父节点取值的条件概率的乘积。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：不会拒绝任何样本，解决了 </span></span>`P(e)` 很小的问题。

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：当证据变量很多时，权重会集中在少数样本上，效率仍然不高。</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">c) MCMC（马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛）</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">过程</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过一个“随机游走”的马尔可夫链来生成样本。每一步只根据</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">马尔可夫毯</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 来采样一个变量的值。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">马尔可夫毯</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：一个变量的父节点、子节点、以及子节点的其他父节点。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：最终会收敛到真实的 posterior 分布，特别适用于复杂网络。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：难以判断何时收敛（“燃烧期”问题）。</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考试可能考察</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简答题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：描述拒绝采样、似然加权和MCMC的基本思想。</span></span>
