    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">比较题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：比较三种采样方法的优缺点。</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：给定一个非常小的网络和CPT，进行几步MCMC采样，并计算概率估计。</span></span>

> ```
> 当精确推理太慢时：近似推理的“艺术”
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">对于大型复杂网络，精确计算可能比登天还难。这时我们采用</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">采样</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">——用统计学的方法来</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">估计</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概率。</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 拒绝采样 - “守株待兔”</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">方法</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：不停地根据模型生成随机可能世界（样本），但只记录那些与现有证据相符的样本，然后在这些“合格”样本里统计比例。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：如果证据本身很罕见（比如 </span></span> $P(警报响)$  很小），那你就像在干草堆里找针，**大部分时间都在生成无效样本并丢弃它们**，效率极低。
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 似然加权 - “精挑细选”</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">方法</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：我们不傻等。我们</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">强制</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">证据发生（如固定 </span></span> $Sprinkler=true$ ），然后生成其他变量。但这样的样本有“偏见”，所以我们给它一个**权重**来纠正这个偏见。这个权重就是“这个样本能出现我们强制设定的证据的可能性有多大”。
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">比喻</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：不是随机抓人来调查，而是专门去找那些符合某个条件（如“养猫”）的人，但在分析时，根据他们代表总体的程度（“权重”）来调整他们的票数。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：不浪费任何样本。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：如果证据很多且苛刻，那么大部分样本的权重都会很小，估计值会由少数几个高权重样本主导，不稳定。</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">c) MCMC - “随机游走”</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">方法</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这不是独立地生成每个样本。而是在网络所有可能的状态空间里进行一场</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">“随机游走”</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。每一步，你只随机改变一个变量的值（根据其马尔可夫毯），从而从一个状态“漫步”到另一个相似的状态。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">为什么有效</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：虽然每一步都是随机的，但只要你走得足够久，你访问每个状态的频率就会稳定下来，而这个</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">频率正好等于该状态的后验概率</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">比喻</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：你不是在随机采访街上的人，而是在一个社区里漫无目的地散步，记录下你看到每家每户在家的次数。散的时间足够长，你就能估计出每家人在家的概率。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：非常适合复杂、多连通的网络，是目前最强大的近似推理方法之一。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">不知道什么时候才算“走得足够久”</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">（收敛性问题）。</span></span>
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 总结与考试提示
> ```
>
> | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">推理方法</span>** | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">核心思想</span>**      | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">优点</span>**     | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">缺点</span>**       | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">考试可能考察</span>**      |
> | ---------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------- |
> | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">枚举法</span>**  | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">列出所有可能情况并求和</span>   | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">概念简单，精确</span>    | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">计算复杂度高，效率低</span>   | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">写出推理公式</span>          |
> | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">变量消除</span>** | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">从右向左求和，缓存中间结果</span> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">比枚举法高效，精确</span>  | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">最坏情况下仍是指数级</span>   | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">描述过程，识别无关变量</span>     |
> | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">拒绝采样</span>** | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">生成样本，拒绝与证据不符的</span> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">简单，一致估计</span>    | $P(e)$ 小时效率极低                                            | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">描述过程，计算估计值</span>      |
> | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">似然加权</span>** | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">固定证据，为样本赋权重</span>   | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">不浪费样本，一致估计</span> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">证据多时权重集中，不稳定</span> | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">描述过程，计算样本权重</span>** |
> | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">MCMC</span>** | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">在状态空间中随机游走</span>    | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">适用于复杂网络，强大</span> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">收敛难判断，可能慢</span>    | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)">描述核心思想（马尔可夫毯采样）</span> |
>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">给初学者的最终建议：</span></span>**
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">理解变量消除</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：它是精确推理的标杆，理解了它就理解了贝叶斯网络推理的本质。</span></span>
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">掌握似然加权</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这是最容易理解和考试的近似推理方法，一定要会计算样本权重。</span></span>
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">理解MCMC的直观</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：你不需要记住算法的每个细节，但要明白它“随机游走”的核心思想以及它为什么有效。</span></span>
>
> 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">明确问题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：遇到推理问题，先问自己是需要精确解还是近似解，再根据网络复杂度和证据情况选择合适的算法。</span></span>

***

```
第七节课 19.2_Supervised_Learning
```

> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">本课围绕</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">从数据中学习</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的核心展开，探索智能体如何从经验中自我进化。内容可分为四大递进模块：</span></span>
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">为什么要学习？</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：确立学习是智能在</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">未知环境中生存与发展</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的根本驱动力。</span></span>
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习的分类</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：描绘出智能探索世界的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">三条核心路径</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">——有导师指导、自主探索与奖惩驱动。</span></span>
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">监督学习</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：深入探讨在“标准答案”指导下，如何从具体数据中</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">抽象出通用规律</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
> 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">神经网络</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：揭示如何通过联结简单的计算单元，构建出能</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">自动学习特征</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的强大模型。</span></span>
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这四大模块的递进，本质上是在重演一遍</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">智能体认知能力的史诗级跃迁</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。你学习的不是一个个孤立的算法，而是在亲历“学习”本身如何从对环境的基本适应，一步步走向高度复杂的自主认知。</span></span>
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">因此，这堂课不仅仅关于机器学习，它更是一个蓝图，向你展示</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">数据如何转化为知识，知识又如何催生智能</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。这一部分对于学习CS5489和CS5487的同样至关重要，这节课就是这两节</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">机器学习的总纲</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，它揭示了那些复杂的函数与功能是如何相互配合作为“神经元”构成复杂的“神经网络”。</span></span>

# **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">一. 为什么要学习？（Why Learning?）</span></span>**

> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习的必要性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">环境的不确定性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> + </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">设计者的局限性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> → </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">需要自适应系统</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心洞见</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：学习不是可选功能，而是智能体在复杂未知环境中生存和发展的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">基本能力</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">三大理由</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">应对未知环境</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：设计者无法预知所有情况，学习让系统自主适应</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">系统构建方法</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过"暴露于现实"而非"手工编码"来构建复杂系统</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优化决策机制</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过学习持续改进智能体的决策性能</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习元素设计</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">性能元素</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：执行任务的组件（如分类器、规划器）</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习元素</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：根据反馈调整知识表示</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">批评器</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：提供性能反馈信号</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">问题生成器</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：主动探索和实验</span></span>

> ```
> 为什么需要学习？（学习的意义）
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">想象一下，你不是在编程，而是在教一个婴儿或者一个机器人。</span></span>
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">应对未知</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：你无法预测未来会发生所有事情（比如路上突然出现一个小水坑）。学习让智能体在遇到没教过的情况时，自己能想办法应对。</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心：让AI适应你没想过的情况。</span></span>**
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">更好的建造方式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：与其像一个程序员一样，苦思冥想写下成千上万条“如果...那么...”的规则（比如：如果看到猫，那么它是动物；如果看到狗，那么它是动物...），不如直接给AI看大量猫、狗、汽车的图片，让它自己总结出规律。</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心：让数据教AI，而不是全靠人教。</span></span>**
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">自我优化</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：学习能让AI在实践中不断调整自己的“想法”和“行为”，越变越聪明。比如一个下棋AI，通过和自己下棋（学习），可以发现新的策略，从而提升棋力。</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心：AI能自己改进自己。</span></span>**
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">一句话总结：学习让AI变得更灵活、更自动、更强大。</span></span>**
>
> ```
> 学习元素的设计（学习的组件）
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这部分描述了一个“学习型智能体”的内部工作流程。我们用一个</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学下棋的AI</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">来类比：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">性能元素</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这是AI</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">当前的本事</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。它就是那个直接下棋的程序，根据当前的棋盘局面，决定下一步走哪里。它依赖现有的“知识”（比如评估函数）。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">批评器</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这是一个</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">裁判</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。它根据一个“性能标准”（比如：赢了还是输了？占了多少优势？）来给</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">性能元素</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的表现打分。这个打分就是“反馈”。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习元素</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这是AI的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">大脑和教练</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。它接收来自</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">批评器</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的反馈（“上一步走错了，导致输了”），然后根据这个反馈去修改</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">性能元素</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">所用的“知识”（比如调整评估函数的参数）。它的目标是提高未来的表现。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">问题生成器</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这是一个</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">好奇心引擎</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。为了避免在已知领域里打转，它会主动提议尝试一些新的、有挑战性的走法（“实验”），比如“试试弃子进攻”，以此来探索新的知识，收集新的反馈。</span></span>
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 它们如何协作？
> ```
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">性能元素</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 去下棋。</span></span>
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">批评器</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 判断这盘棋下得好不好，给出</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">反馈</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。</span></span>
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习元素</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 根据反馈，修改</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">性能元素</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的知识，让它下次表现得更好。</span></span>
>
> 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">问题生成器</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 提议尝试新策略，加速学习过程。</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">下方表格的例子</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">是为了告诉你，这个“学习框架”可以应用在各种不同的任务上：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">下棋</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：反馈是“输/赢”。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">逻辑规划</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：反馈是“行动导致了什么结果”。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">医疗监控</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：反馈是“监测到的新数据”。</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">图像分类</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：反馈是“这张图正确的标签是什么”。</span></span>

# **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">二. 学习的分类（Categories of Learning）</span></span>**

> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习的三条进化路径</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">有导师指导</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> vs </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">自主探索</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> vs </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">奖惩驱动</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心区别</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：监督信号的形式和时机决定了学习范式的本质差异</span></span>

![\<img alt="" data-attachment-key="XU8BAMGV" width="1262" height="391" src="attachments/XU8BAMGV.png" ztype="zimage"> | 1262](attachments/XU8BAMGV.png)

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 监督学习（Supervised Learning）</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">定义</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：从</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">带标签</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的训练样本中学习输入到输出的映射</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">关键特征</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：每个训练样本都有明确的"正确答案"</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">类比</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：如同学生有标准答案的练习题</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">典型任务</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：分类、回归</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 无监督学习（Unsupervised Learning）</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">定义</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：从</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">无标签</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">数据中发现内在结构和模式</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">关键特征</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：没有外部指导，完全自主探索</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">类比</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：如同科学家从原始数据中发现自然规律</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">典型任务</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：聚类、降维、关联规则挖掘</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">c) 强化学习（Reinforcement Learning）</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">定义</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">试错</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">和</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">延迟奖励</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习最优策略</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">关键特征</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：只有稀疏的奖励信号，没有直接指导</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">类比</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：如同婴儿学步，通过摔倒和站起来的反馈学习</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">典型任务</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：游戏AI、机器人控制、资源调度</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考试可能考察</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">分类题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：给定具体问题，判断最适合的学习范式</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">比较题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：对比三种学习范式的训练信号差异</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">应用题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：为特定场景选择合适的学习方法并说明理由</span></span>

# **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">三. 监督学习（Supervised Learning）</span></span>**

> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">监督学习</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">训练数据（带标签）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> + </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习算法</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> → </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">预测模型</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心目标</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：从带标签的训练集中学习一个未知目标函数 𝑓，得到能在新数据上准确预测的假设 ℎ</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 基本概念与流程</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">训练集</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> ${(x_i, y_i)}$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">，其中 </span></span> $y_i = f(x_i)$

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">假设 ℎ</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：学习到的函数，目标是 </span></span> $h ≈ f$

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">监督学习流程</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    1.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">准备带标签数据</span></span>

    2.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">选择假设空间 </span></span> $H$

    3.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">确定拟合度度量</span></span>

    4.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习最优假设 </span></span> $h$

    5.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">在测试集上评估</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 两大任务类型</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">分类</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：输出离散值（如是否购买保险）</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">评估指标</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：准确率、精确率、召回率、F1分数</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">回归</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：输出连续值（如房价预测）</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">评估指标</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：均方误差、平均绝对误差</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">c) 关键挑战与解决方案</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">过拟合 vs 欠拟合</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">欠拟合</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：模型过于简单，训练和测试误差都高</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">过拟合</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：模型过于复杂，训练误差低但测试误差高</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">正则化技术</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">岭回归（L2）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $E(w) = \frac{1}{2}\sum(h(x_n)-y_n)^2 + \frac{\lambda}{2}||w||^2$

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Lasso回归（L1）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $E(w) = \frac{1}{2}\sum(h(x_n)-y_n)^2 + \frac{\lambda}{2}||w||_1$

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考试可能考察</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：计算给定模型的损失函数，包括正则化项</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">分析题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：诊断模型是过拟合还是欠拟合，并提出改进方案</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">设计题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：为具体问题设计完整的监督学习流程</span></span>

> ```
> 我们要解决什么问题？
> ```
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">监督学习就像</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">跟着菜谱学做菜</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">训练数据</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = 别人做好的美味菜肴（带标签的示例）</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习算法</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = 你观察和分析这些菜肴的方法</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">模型</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = 你总结出的做菜规律</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">预测</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = 按照你总结的规律自己做新菜</span></span>
>
> <!---->
>
> ```
> 分类模型详解
> ```
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">1. 决策树</span></span>**
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">基本思想</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过一系列 if-then 规则进行分类</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">构建算法</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> 1.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">选择"最佳"分裂属性（基于信息增益）</span></span>
> 2.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">为该节点分配决策属性</span></span>
> 3.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">为每个属性值创建子节点</span></span>
> 4.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">将训练样本分配到叶节点</span></span>
> 5.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">如果完美分类则停止，否则递归处理新叶节点</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">信息增益计算</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">熵：</span></span> $I(p) = -(p_1\log p_1 + p_2\log p_2 + \cdots + p_n\log p_n)$
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">信息增益 = 父节点熵 - 子节点加权平均熵</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">例子分析</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：<br>通过计算Area、Income、Child三个属性的信息增益，发现Child的信息增益最大(0.5488)，因此首先按Child属性分裂。</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">过拟合防范</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">限制树高度</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">统计显著性检验</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">获取更多训练数据</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">使用验证集选择最优树</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优点：快速简单、可转为规则、处理噪声数据</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点：单变量分裂、大树难理解、需要全部数据</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">2. 逻辑回归</span></span>**
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">假设空间</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：线性决策边界<br></span></span>$H=\{w∣h(w,x)=w_0+w_1x(1)+⋯+w_mx(m)=w^Tx\}$
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Sigmoid函数</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：将输出映射到[0,1]<br></span></span>$σ(z)=\frac{1}{1+e^{−z}}$
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">交叉熵损失</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：<br></span></span>$E(w)=\frac{1}{2}\sum_{n=1}^{N}[−y_n\log⁡ σ(w^Tx_n)−(1−y_n)\log⁡(1−σ(w^Tx_n))]$
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">梯度下降</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：<br></span></span>$\frac{∂E(w)}{∂w_i}=\sum_{n=1}^N[σ(w^Tx_n)−y_n]x_{ni}$
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优点：易扩展到多类、不需全部数据、训练快、简单数据集效果好</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点：线性决策边界</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">3. 支持向量机(SVM)</span></span>**
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">线性SVM</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：寻找最大间隔超平面</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优化目标</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">最小化：</span></span> $\frac{1}{2}||w||^2$
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">约束：</span></span> $y_n(w^Tx_n + w_0) \geq 1, \forall n$
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">非线性SVM</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过核函数 </span></span>$\phi(x)$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 映射到高维空间<br></span></span>$H=\{w∣h(w,x)=w^Tϕ(x)\}$
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优点：泛化能力强、支持非线性、高维鲁棒</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点：不适合大数据集、核函数选择困难</span></span>
>
> > ```
> > 三大分类模型的"个性特点"
> > ```
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 决策树 - "直白的检查官"</span></span>**
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">工作方式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：像查户口一样，一个一个条件问下去</span></span>
> >
> >     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">"有孩子吗？" → "没有" → "收入高吗？" → "高" → "会买保险"</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">优点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：决策过程透明，容易理解</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">缺点</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：问题问得太死板，不够灵活</span></span>
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 逻辑回归 - "温和的评分员"</span></span>**
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">工作方式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：不直接给答案，而是给一个"可能性分数"</span></span>
> >
> >     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">"根据你的情况，买保险的可能性是73%"</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心工具</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：Sigmoid函数，把分数变成概率</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习方式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过梯度下降不断调整"评分标准"</span></span>
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">c) 支持向量机 - "严格的边界守卫"</span></span>**
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">工作方式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：在两个类别之间画一条"最宽的安全带"</span></span>
> >
> >     *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">尽量让两个类别离分界线都远远的</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">升级版</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：当数据绕来绕去时，用"核技巧"把数据映射到高维空间再划分</span></span>
>
> ```
> 过拟合：机器学习中的"死记硬背"
> ```
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">什么是过拟合</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">好学生</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：理解原理，遇到新题也会做</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">过拟合学生</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：把练习题答案背下来，但遇到新题就傻眼</span></span>
>
> > ```
> > CS5489   Lecture 2.2: Logistic Regression
> > ```
> >
> > <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">单纯追求训练数据上的似然最大，可能导致</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">过拟合</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">。模型可能会学到一些数据中的噪声和极端特性，使得 </span></span>$w $ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">的某些值变得非常大，从而降低泛化能力。</span><span style="background-color: rgba(241, 152, 55, 0.5)">我们不是寻找“最可能产生数据”的参数，而是寻找“在给定数据下最可能”的参数。</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">过拟合现象</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">： 一个过拟合的模型就像是一个死记硬背了所有考题答案的学生。它</span><span style="background-color: rgba(255, 212, 0, 0.5)">在训练集上表现近乎完美，但在遇到新的、没见过的题目（测试集）时表现糟糕。</span><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">这是因为模型不仅学到了数据中普遍的规律，还学到了训练数据中特有的噪声和随机波动。</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">解决方法</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">正则化</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：给模型"减肥"，防止它记住太多细节</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">交叉验证</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：用模拟考试来检查真实水平</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简化模型</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：用更简单的模型避免过度复杂</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">4. 模型选择指南</span></span>**
>
> | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">模型</span></span>** | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">适用场景</span></span>**  | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">好比</span></span>** | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">注意事项</span></span>** |
> | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">决策树</span></span>    | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">需要解释性的场景</span></span>  | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">流程图</span></span>    | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">容易过度生长</span></span>   |
> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">逻辑回归</span></span>   | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概率预测、线性问题</span></span> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">评分卡</span></span>    | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">只能处理线性关系</span></span> |
> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">SVM</span></span>    | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">小数据集、复杂边界</span></span> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">最佳分界线</span></span>  | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">大数据集计算慢</span></span>  |
>
>
> ***
>
> ```
> 总结与考试提示
> ```
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心概念掌握</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">理解监督学习的基本流程和数据流向</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">掌握过拟合/欠拟合的识别和解决方法</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">熟悉三大分类模型的核心思想</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">典型考题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：计算信息增益、梯度下降更新</span></span>
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">分析题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：诊断模型问题并提出改进方案</span></span>
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">比较题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：对比不同模型的优缺点和适用场景</span></span>
>
> 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">设计题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：为具体问题设计完整的解决方案</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">给初学者的最终建议</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">理解决策树</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这是最直观的模型，理解了它就理解了机器学习的基本思想</span></span>
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">掌握逻辑回归</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这是很多复杂模型的基础，梯度下降的思想贯穿整个深度学习</span></span>
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">了解SVM的直观</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：理解"最大间隔"和"核技巧"的核心思想</span></span>
>
> 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">重视过拟合问题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这是实践中最常见也最重要的问题</span></span>

# **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">四. 神经网络（Neural Networks）</span></span>**

> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">神经网络</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> = </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">生物启发</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> + </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">数学抽象</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> → </span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">万能函数逼近器</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心思想</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过多层非线性变换，从简单特征中自动学习复杂特征表示</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">a) 神经元与激活函数</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">McCulloch-Pitts神经元</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $y_k = \varphi(\sum_j W_{kj}x_j)$

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">激活函数家族</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Sigmoid</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $\varphi(x) = \frac{1}{1+e^{-x}}$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">（平滑，易饱和）</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Tanh</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $\varphi(x) = \tanh(x)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">（零中心化）</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">ReLU</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $\varphi(x) = \max(0, x)$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">（计算简单，缓解梯度消失）</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">b) 网络架构演进</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">单层感知机</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：只能解决线性可分问题（AND, OR）</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">多层感知机（MLP）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过隐藏层解决非线性问题（XOR）</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">表达能力</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：理论上，单隐藏层MLP可以逼近任何连续函数</span></span>

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">c) 训练算法：反向传播</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">前向传播</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：计算网络输出和损失</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">反向传播</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：利用链式法则计算梯度<br></span></span> $\frac{\partial E}{\partial w_i} = \frac{\partial E}{\partial y} \cdot \frac{\partial y}{\partial o} \cdot \frac{\partial o}{\partial w_i}$

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">权重更新</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $w_i ← w_i - \alpha \frac{\partial E}{\partial w_i}$

## **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">d) 深度学习架构</span></span>**

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">卷积神经网络（CNN）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">卷积层</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：局部连接，权重共享，提取空间特征</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">池化层</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：降维，增强平移不变性</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">应用</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：图像分类、目标检测</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">循环神经网络（RNN）</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">记忆机制</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span> $h_t = \omega\varphi(h_{t-1}) + \omega_x x_t$

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">序列建模</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：处理时间序列、自然语言</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">应用</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：文本生成、股票预测</span></span>

*   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">考试可能考察</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">推导题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：推导反向传播的梯度计算公式</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">设计题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：为具体任务设计合适的神经网络架构</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">分析题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：分析不同激活函数的优缺点及适用场景</span></span>

    *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">概念题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：解释CNN中卷积和池化操作的作用</span></span>

> ```
> 神经网络的生物灵感
> ```
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">1. 生物神经元</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">规模</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：人脑由约 </span></span> $10^{11}$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 个神经元、</span></span> $10^{14}$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"> 个突触构成</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">工作方式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：树突接收电信号，轴突发送信号</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">循环时间</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：1-10毫秒</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">2. 大脑 vs 人工神经网络</span></span>**
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">相似之处</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">都有神经元和连接</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">学习 = 改变连接强度，而非改变神经元本身</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">大规模并行处理</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">人工网络的简化</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">神经元内部计算极大简化</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">离散时间步骤</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">通常采用监督学习+大量刺激</span></span>
>
> > ```
> > 神经网络的"进化史"
> > ```
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">第一阶段：模仿生物（单神经元）</span></span>**
> >
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">就像只用一个脑细胞思考，只能做最简单的是非判断</span></span>
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">第二阶段：团队协作（单层感知机）</span></span>**
> >
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">多个脑细胞一起工作，能处理复杂一点的问题</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">局限</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：像一群人但没人当领导，还是解决不了复杂问题</span></span>
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">第三阶段：建立管理层（多层感知机）</span></span>**
> >
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">有了"中层管理"，能处理非线性问题</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">突破</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：终于能解决XOR这种"非此即彼又非彼非此"的复杂逻辑</span></span>
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">第四阶段：专业分工（CNN/RNN）</span></span>**
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">CNN</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：像视觉专家，专门处理图像</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">RNN</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：像记忆大师，专门处理序列</span></span>
>
> ```
> 从单神经元到多层网络
> ```
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">1. McCulloch-Pitts神经元</span></span>**
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">基本公式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>$y_k = \varphi(\sum_j W_{kj}x_j)$
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心思想</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">对真实神经元的极度简化</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">输出是输入信号的"压缩"线性函数</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">奠定了理解简单单元网络能力的基础</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">2. 激活函数家族</span></span>**
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">引入</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">非线性</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">以获得足够的表达能力：</span></span>
>
> | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">函数类型</span></span>** | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">公式</span></span>** | **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">特点</span></span>**      |
> | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">阶跃函数</span></span>     | $\varphi(x) = \begin{cases} 1, & x \geq 0 \ 0, & x < 0 \end{cases}$                                          | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">最简单，不连续</span></span>     |
> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Sigmoid</span></span>  | $\varphi(x) = \frac{1}{1+e^{-x}}$                                                                            | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">平滑，易饱和</span></span>      |
> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Tanh</span></span>     | $\varphi(x) = \tanh x$                                                                                       | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">零中心化</span></span>        |
> | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">ReLU</span></span>     | $\varphi(x) = \max(0, x)$                                                                                    | <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算简单，缓解梯度消失</span></span> |
>
>
> > ```
> > 激活函数：神经网络的"性格"
> > ```
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">阶跃函数</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：非黑即白，决断力强但太死板</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">Sigmoid</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：温和派，什么都给个概率值</span></span>
> >
> > *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">ReLU</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：实用主义，负输入直接归零，正输入原样输出</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">3. 单层感知机</span></span>**
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">结构</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：最简单的神经网络</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">限制</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：各输出独立操作，无共享权重</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">表达能力</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：只能表示线性可分问题（AND, OR），无法解决XOR问题</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">决策边界</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>$w_1x_1 + w_2x_2 + b \geq 0$
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">4. 多层感知机(MLP)</span></span>**
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">突破</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：通过隐藏层引入更多非线性</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">网络结构</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">通常全连接</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">隐藏单元数量通常手动选择</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">输出：</span></span> $y = \varphi[w_1\varphi(w_{11}x_1 + w_{21}x_2) + w_2\varphi(w_{12}x_1 + w_{22}x_2) + w_3\varphi(w_{13}x_1 + w_{23}x_2)]$
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">解决XOR问题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">定义平方损失：</span></span> $E(w) = \frac{1}{2}\sum_{n=1}^N (\hat{y}^n - y^n)^2$
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">权重初始化为1</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">通过梯度下降更新：</span></span> $w ← w - \alpha \frac{\partial E(w)}{\partial w}$
>
> ### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">神经网络训练机制</span></span>**
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">1. 链式法则求导</span></span>**
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">通过反向传播计算梯度：</span></span>
>
> $$
> \frac{\partial E\left(w_{i}\right)}{\partial w_{i}}=\frac{\partial E\left(w_{i}\right)}{\partial y^{n}} \cdot \frac{\partial y^{n}}{\partial o^{n}} \cdot \frac{\partial o^{n}}{\partial w_{i}}
> $$
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">2. 前向传播</span></span>**
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算网络输出：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">输入 → 隐藏层计算 → 输出层计算 → 预测值</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">示例：对于输入(1,1)，经过sigmoid激活，得到预测输出0.9335</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">3. 反向传播</span></span>**
>
> <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">根据误差调整权重：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">从输出层向输入层逐层传播误差</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">使用链式法则计算每个权重的梯度</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">更新权重：</span></span> $w_i = w_i - \alpha \frac{\partial E(w_i)}{\partial w_i}$
>
> > ```
> > 反向传播：神经网络的"学习方式"
> > ```
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">好比学骑自行车</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
> >
> > 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">前向传播</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：试骑一下，看摔没摔</span></span>
> >
> > 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算误差</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：分析为什么摔了（车把歪了？重心偏了？）</span></span>
> >
> > 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">反向传播</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：把误差原因一层层传回去</span></span>
> >
> > 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">调整权重</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：根据原因调整动作（下次少歪一点车把）</span></span>
>
> ```
> 深度学习架构
> ```
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">1. 从MLP到深度学习</span></span>**
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心思想</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：更多层 = 更深的学习能力</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">2. 卷积神经网络(CNN)</span></span>**
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">解决图像问题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">问题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：1000×1000图像连接100万隐藏单元 → 10亿参数！</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">解决方案</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：卷积神经网络</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">CNN的核心创新</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">局部连接</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：空间相关性是局部的</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">参数共享</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：在不同位置使用相同参数</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">参数减少</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：从10亿参数减少到1万参数（使用100个10×10滤波器）</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">卷积操作</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">滤波器（核）在输入上滑动</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">卷积和进入特征图</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">滤波器参数是需要学习的</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">池化层</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">目的</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：使学习特征对模式精确位置不敏感</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">效果</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：进一步减少特征维度</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">示例</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：最大池化（2×2滤波器，步长2）</span></span>
>
