> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">典型CNN架构</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：<br>输入图像 → 卷积 → 非线性 → 空间池化 → 归一化 → 特征图 → 全连接输出\</span></span>
>
> > ```
> > CNN：图像处理的"火眼金睛"
> > ```
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">为什么需要CNN</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
> >
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">全连接网络看图像就像"数头发"：太细致反而看不到整体</span></span>
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">CNN看图像就像"看森林"：先看局部特征，再组合成整体</span></span>
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">卷积的直观理解</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
> >
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">像用一个"小探照灯"在图像上滑动</span></span>
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">每个"探照灯"学习寻找特定模式（边缘、角点等）</span></span>
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">池化的作用</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
> >
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">像"模糊记忆"：记得这里有个眼睛，但不记得精确位置</span></span>
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">让模型对微小变化不敏感，提高泛化能力</span></span>
>
> #### **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">3. 循环神经网络(RNN)</span></span>**
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">处理序列数据</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">适用场景</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：文本生成、股价预测等序列数据</span></span>
>
> *   **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">与传统NN区别</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：传统网络输入输出大小固定</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">RNN核心结构</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   $x_t$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：时间t的输入</span></span>
>
> *   $h_t$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：时间t的隐藏状态（记忆）</span></span>
>
> *   $y_t$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：时间t的输出</span></span>
>
> *   $w, w_x, w_y$ <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：在不同时间步保持相同的权重</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">公式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：<br></span></span>$h_t=ωφ(h_{t−1})+ω_xx_t$<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)"><br></span></span>$y_t=ω_yφ(h_t)$
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">展开的RNN</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">可视为同一网络的多个副本</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">每个时间步使用相同的函数和参数集</span></span>
> *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">每个网络将消息传递给后继者</span></span>
>
> > ```
> > NN：有"记忆力"的网络
> > ```
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">传统网络</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：像金鱼，只有7秒记忆<br></span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">RNN</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：像正常人，能记住前面说了什么</span></span>
> >
> > **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">工作方式</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
> >
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">不仅看当前输入，还参考之前的"记忆"</span></span>
> > *   <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">适合处理一句话、一段音乐、股价序列等</span></span>
>
> ```
> 总结与考试提示
> ```
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">核心概念掌握</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> 1.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">理解从单神经元到深度网络的演进逻辑</span></span>
> 2.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">掌握不同激活函数的特性和适用场景</span></span>
> 3.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">理解反向传播的链式法则思想</span></span>
> 4.  <span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">掌握CNN和RNN解决特定问题的原理</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">典型考题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">计算题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：前向传播计算、梯度计算</span></span>
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">简答题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：解释CNN的局部连接和参数共享</span></span>
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">分析题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：为什么单层感知机不能解决XOR问题</span></span>
>
> 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">设计题</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：为具体任务选择合适的网络架构</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">给初学者的学习路径</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
>
> 1.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">先理解单神经元</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：这是所有复杂网络的基础</span></span>
>
> 2.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">掌握激活函数</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：理解非线性变换的重要性</span></span>
>
> 3.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">理解决策边界</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：明白网络如何做分类</span></span>
>
> 4.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">理解反向传播直觉</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：不必死记公式，理解思想更重要</span></span>
>
> 5.  **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">区分CNN/RNN应用场景</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：知道什么时候用什么网络</span></span>
>
> **<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">最终目标</span></span>**<span style="color: rgb(15, 17, 21)"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255)">：</span></span>
